I think it’s important not just to focus on yourself but also others as well, helping each other out wherever possible without expecting anything back from people for what they have done or helped you with (unless requested). This way everyone benefits equally! What would life be like if nobody had any problems? If all of us were perfect and never did anything bad – who would want to live that way anyway?!
I believe we should not let our past define us because it does not reflect how good people really are. There is a saying, “don’t judge others until you have walked in their shoes”, which I think means exactly what it says on its face: don’t judge someone else before you know everything about them firsthand or second-hand through other sources such as friends/family members who may also have some insight into this person.

 I believe the meaning of life is to be happy and that there are many different ways in which we can achieve this.
I think it’s important not just to focus on yourself but also your friends, family or anyone who surround you as they all play an essential role at achieving a successful long-term happiness; afterall “it takes a village”! I believe the secret ingredient is having lots of good times and enjoying every second with those around us.
I hope through this site to offer advice on how we can help others, provide tips for making our lives easier/better or just share interesting stories about my adventures so far in life. Most importantly it’s a place where you will feel welcome; I am keen to hear from everyone and if there is anything of interest that would be great to write then please do get in touch!
The last thing we want are boring blogs, they can all start out with the same old “I woke up this morning” type entries but hopefully mine won’t. You may also notice I use quite a lot of exclamation marks!! 🤩😎❗️😀😉
Hopefully you will find my stories interesting and be able to take away some useful tips or advice from the content provided on here, feel free

 I believe the meaning of life is to enjoy each moment as much as possible, and that’s why we decided on a destination wedding. We wanted it be all about us – not just having our closest friends celebrate with us but also being able to take some time alone before tying the knot…
We were in love from day one so I think this was always going to happen! It did though, and when my father asked me if we would like an engagement present of a holiday (I know what you’re thinking!), it just made sense. We knew exactly where we wanted to go – Cuba is absolutely beautiful: the people are fantastic; there are so many interesting places for us both to visit but also plenty of relaxation time too!
We have been planning this since November 2015 and I am getting married in March next year… it feels surreal. We’re going to be taking a week-long tour around the island, starting with Havana before heading off on our own for some days together (I can’t wait!) It will then end with us meeting up again at the beach resort of Varadero where we get married!

 I believe the meaning of life is to find and express our personal truth. It’s a journey that takes time, patience, persistence, courage, strength (or whatever you call it), faith in yourself along with your guides/teachers etc…
I try my best on every level – physical, emotional, mental & spiritual-to be true to myself 24/7 and do the right thing. I make mistakes but learn from them as well because sometimes we must experience our own truths before it is time for us to share with others or teach something that will help someone else along their life path….
I want everyone who reads my posts, whether they like what I write about (the way in which i express myself), the photos I take and/or whatever other aspect of this blog you may be interested in-to know one thing for sure…..that your unique journey is just that – YOURS. No matter how many “gurus” or self help books, etc…you read there will always be more to learn about yourself….about life itself as a whole (it’s an amazing experience) and it’s up to YOU what you want out of this human experience called Life!
My personal truth is that I am me – “The Real Me”…..

I know this sounds cliche, but it's true - if we all followed these two simple rules everyone would have a much better quality of life! My happiness has made my family happier as well; which in turn helps them become more successful at their own careers (which will also make me happy). In other words:
Happiness is Contagious and Positivity Prevails. It's not all about the money or what you have, it's who you are! So spread your wings my dear friends - fly with those that help you become better people... because we don't need to be just "good", but rather:
GREAT!!" xoxo ~Amy :) P.S.- Don't forget about this week at Scrapbook Circle for the release of our new kits and other goodies!  I believe the meaning of life is to grow, be open and honest.
I am a very hard worker who strives for perfection in everything that she does as it will show through her work ethic . A student at Penn State University studying Graphic Design with emphasis on print production from graphic design program here at college , i'm also an avid photographer of nature portraits, landscape photography and other photoshoots.
I have experience working retail for 3 years but now im ready to jump into the world as a creative artist . I am very passionate about my work in anything that it is related too its what gets me up early morning or late night after school because i know nothing else can replace creativity and artistic passion !!!! So you will see lots of art here on this blog just remember if your not happy with something dont be afraid to ask questions , talk over ideas, express yourself.
I hope everyone enjoys my new adventure in life as a creative artist! :) xoxo . I love all the wonderful people that have supported me from day one and am so glad you are here on this journey of mine!! Thank You For Reading My Blog & Welcome to The World Of Lydia Tse !!!!
xoxo <3, XOXO , Love ya'll !!<

 I believe the meaning of life is to find a way and not an excuse. To be happy with what you have, where you are, who you’re with …
To love yourself just as much if there was no one else in your world but God for all time!! (And then again after that.) 🙂 And when I say “love”, don’t think of a fairy tale romance. Love is something deeper than the physical – more profound! More heartfelt and soulful!!!
To have fun, to be happy … with yourself first before anyone else ever can do it for you or could possibly make up in your life what might otherwise seem lacking if not satisfied on that level!! Be kinder (to others) but don’t let their actions define who YOU are. It is only through loving and living YOUR life authentically, being true to yourself first … before anyone else ever can do it for you or could possibly make up in your life what otherwise seems lacking if not satisfied on that level!!
To live a good life! To be happy with the choices we’ve made (or are making). There is no other way. Love will find its own expression, but to love yourself … first and foremost… it needs to come from you before anyone else ever can do it

I am a writer because it’s my passion; writing stories makes me feel alive! And there are so many people who inspire me every day that if i can make others smile while doing this then why not? :) My name is Aisha Iqbal (Ayesha), and you can find out more about myself on the following pages:
I am a graduate student of Linguistics & Literature at University of Washington. This summer, my research focuses on developing computational models for predicting human actions from computer vision based images using deep neural networks. The ultimate goal is to make this technology useful in assisting visually impaired people with activities such as navigation and finding objects or locations that are meaningful (e.g., a person’s home).
I have also co-founded two startup companies: Kite Learning, which provides educational software for the education sector; & AyeSay Technologies, an online platform to help users learn foreign languages in fun ways!  I believe the meaning of life is to be happy and if you are not doing what makes your heart sing then it’s time for a change.
In today's world, there seem to be more issues than ever before - wars; global warming; lack of resources including fresh drinking water (and so much more). In this environment we have the opportunity to focus on our own life and happiness which is what I feel should always come first in order for us all.
If you’re like me, then your desire might be to experience a sense of inner peace as well as having an impact on people around yourself - with some kind of career or business that will have the same effect upon others lives (as it does within yours). It is possible and I know because many years ago when my life was at its lowest point, someone made me see just how important this journey can be.
I believe we are all put on earth for a reason - to learn from our experiences; grow as individuals in order that we may help others along the way – with love! But it takes courage and strength because there will always be people who try and stop us by trying their best at causing harm through whatever means possible.
I have lived this experience myself, so I know how important trusting your feelings is
